interface IAnimal {
run(): void;
}

class Dog implements IAnimal {
gav() {}
run() {}
}

class Cat implements IAnimal {
mew() { }
run() {}
}

const animals = [new Cat, new Cat, new Dog]

const a = {
Mew(animal: Cat) {
animal.mew()
}
}
function mew(animal: Cat) {
animal.mew()
}

animals.forEach((animal: Cat) => {
animal.mew()
});
animals.forEach(function (animal: Cat) {
animal.mew()
});
animals.forEach(a.Mew);
animals.forEach(mew);
